text: "MELODEON.\nAnd gladly wander up and down,\nAnd smile at toil and pain.gob\nI suffer on my three-score years,\nTill my Deliverer come,\nAnd wipe away his servant\'s tears,\nAnd take his exile home.\n281\n3 O what hath Jesus bought for me!\nBefore my ravished eyes\nRivers of life divine I see,\nAnd trees of paradise!\nI see a world of spirits bright,\nWho taste the pleasures there;\nThey all are robed in spotless white,\nAnd conq\'ring palms they bear!\nfron Ston\n4 O what are all my sufferings here,\nIf, Lord, thou count me meet v\nWith that enraptured host t\' appear,\nAnd worship at thy feet!\nGive joy or grief, give ease or pain,\nTake life or friends away;\nBut let me find them all again\nIn that eternal day.\nXDU\nHYMN 230.-L. M.\nBLESS\'D Jesus, what delicious fare-\nHow sweet thine entertainments are!"
